කල්තැබීම

ஒத்திைவப்ᾗ ADJOURNMENT ගරු නිමල් සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මහතා ( மாண்ᾗமிகு நிமல் சிறிபால த சில்வா) (The Hon. Nimal Siripala de Silva) ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ''පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව දැන් කල් තැබිය යුතුය'' යි මා ෙයෝජනා කරනවා.

පශ්නය සභාභිමුඛ කරන ලදී. வினா எᾌத்தியம்பப்ெபற்றᾐ. Question proposed.

නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) දැන් සභාව කල් තබන අවස්ථාෙව් ෙයෝජනාව ඉදිරිපත් කිරීම. ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මන්තීතුමා. දවිඩ ජාතිකයන් අත්අඩංගුවට ගැනීම සහ රඳවා තැබීම தமிழர்கள் ைகᾐ ெசய்யப்பᾌதᾤம் தᾌத்ᾐ ைவக்கப்பᾌதᾤம் ARREST AND DETENTION OF TAMILS ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯ காந்தா) (The Hon. N. Sri Kantha) Mr. Deputy Speaker, I am most thankful to you, Sir, and also to this august Assembly for having given me this opportunity to move this Adjournment Motion today of which, I in fact, gave notice in the morning of last Monday the 3rd of December. Now, with your permission, Sir, I move, “Whereas more than a thousand Tamils who were arrested during the last few days by the police and the security forces, are now being detained at several police stations and the Boossa prison on the detention orders issued by the Secretary to the Ministry of Defence, under the Emergency Regulations, without any valid reason whatsoever.

And whereas the said arrests and detentions of those Tamils as aforesaid are in gross violation of the fundamental rights guaranteed to them as citizens of Sri Lanka, under the Constitution and more particularly, Articles 12 and 13. This Parliament resolves that all those citizens who are on detention as aforesaid be released forthwith.” Sir, when I gave notice of this Motion in the morning of last Monday, the figure of those who had been arrested and detained under the Emergency Regulations by virtue of detention orders purported to have been issued under the hand of the Secretary to the Ministry of Defence were in fact over a thousand. I must concede that the number has considerably decreased or rather lessened now and if I go by what the Minister Hon. Jeyaraj Fernandopulle stated yesterday, in the morning, on the Floor of this august Assembly and thereafter in the afternoon or rather in the evening at a press conference, the number concerned stands a little over hundred. Let it be as it is. My contention, Sir, is that these detainees whether the number concerned is hundred, over hundred or two hundred, whatever it may be, are being detained in violation of their fundamental rights guaranteed under the Constitution and more particularly Article 12 and 13. I say so, Sir, for the reason that Article 12(1) states as follows. I quote: “ 12.(1) All persons are equal before the law and are entitled to the equal protection of the law. ” Article 12(2), Sir, states as follows. I quote: “12.(2) No citizen shall be discriminated against on the grounds of race, religion, language, caste, sex, political opinion, place of birth or any one of such grounds:"

2421 2422

2007 ෙදසැම්බර් 05

And there is a proviso to that. Article 13.(1) too on which I rely in regard to my Motion, states as follows. I quote: “ 13.(1) No person shall be arrested except according to procedure established by law. Any person arrested shall be informed of the reason for his arrest." Now, Sir, there is no denying of the fact that on the night of the last Friday and again on Saturday and Sunday there had been indiscriminate arrests of Tamils in the capital City of Colombo and its suburbs and certain other places in the South of Sri Lanka by the police and the armed forces cloaked with the powers under the Emergency Regulations. These are cases of indiscriminate arrests, random arrests without any reason whatsoever. I contend, Sir, that no one single citizen who was arrested was informed of the reason of his or her arrest as the case may be. No receipt was given as mandated under the Emergency Regulations. They were taken to the police stations, kept there and a sizeable number, a significant number were later detained on detention orders issued by the Secretary to the Ministry of Defence. It is my contention, Mr. Deputy Speaker, that out of more than 2500 Tamils or rather citizens, I would prefer to say, who were arrested 98 per cent were Tamils. There may be a few Sinhalese and a few Muslims who might have been picked up on various other grounds or with a view to give a picture as if there has been no discrimination on grounds of race or language or place of birth. But, these persons have been arrested from their houses, from buses and vans in which they were travelling and they were locked up and now, we find more than a hundred detained at Boossa. Mr. Deputy Speaker, there is no denying of the fact that in consequence of various political representations made by certain Hon. Members of this august Assembly belonging to the government, a good number of detainees have already been released. I have no grouse over that. I am really happy about that. But, there are hapless people, helpless people who know of anybody who can influence the government or for that matter the Secretary to the Ministry of Defence, if I could put it in pure legal terms, to have these detention orders revoked. It is my contention that they are being detained unlawfully. They are being detained without any valid grounds whatsoever. One cannot be detained, Mr. Deputy Speaker, with the police or army saying that you are an LTTEer. There is no ground for that. One cannot be arrested with the armed forces or police saying that you have committed an offence under the Emergency Regulations. No. There are a series of Supreme Court decisions, a series of decisions running from that famous case of Rajitha Senaratne, no one other than the Hon. Minister and my good Friend, Rajitha Senaratne versus Punya de Silva case that was decided by the Supreme Court in 1995 and there is the other case, Selvakumar versus Devananda. It was no one other than the Hon. Minister, again my good Friend Douglas Devananda,

which was decided in 1994 by the Supreme Court, which with doubt give to anybody, who can retain his basic sense of sanity, as to how an arrest under the Emergency Regulations should be effected and as to how a Detention Order could be made. But everything had been violated and I find Government officials including Hon. Ministers stating that persons who could not prove their identity were taken into custody and detained. There is no law in this country for detaining a person under the Emergency Regulations for his or her failure to prove his identity. If I do not have an Identity Card then that is a different matter altogether. I cannot be arrested. If I have already applied, got one and lost or did not have it at the time of arrest I cannot be dealt with in such a manner under the law. If I have not applied then that is a different matter altogether. That comes under the Registration of Persons (Amendment) Act, a punishable offence for not having applied and got a National Identity Card. One cannot be detained, Sir, on the whims and fancies of anybody in this country however mighty or powerful he or she may be. That is my contention. I am not on any political ground. I am on constitutional grounds because this concerns fundamental rights, sacred rights, the birth rights of each and every citizen of this country. In this country His Excellency the President is the most powerful, no doubt. He has the powers; Ministers have the powers; Deputy Ministers have the powers; police have the powers; armed forces have the powers. But when it comes to fundamental rights all are equal whether it is His Excellency the President; or for that matter the Hon. Prime Minister for whom I have the highest regards as a noble gentleman; or for that matter my learned Friend, my good Friend, the Hon. Rauff Hakeem; or for that matter my Colleagues of the TNA and, or for that matter an ordinary citizen wearing sarong and smoking a beedi tucking up his sarong and enjoying the free air in any evening on the roads of Colombo or its suburbs or any part of the country including the North and East. All are equal but, it has been violated. It has been violated because they were Tamils. Most of them were from the North and East. Their respective Identity Cards showed that their place of birth was, in fact, the North and East. Some are from the hill country. Just because they happened to be Tamils they have been arrested. My contention, Sir, is that there is no provision under the Emergency Regulations to arrest a person first and detain him later. I repeat. Apparently and obviously these detention orders have been made under Regulation 19, one of the Emergency Regulations dated 13th August 2005. If that is the position the detention orders would show unless tampered with after my contention. It cannot be a lawful law under the law because anybody who could read Regulation 19 (1) - I have a copy of the Emergency Regulations dated 13.08.2005 - would agree with me that the Secretary to the Ministry of Defence by a Detention Order must name the person, ordering the person to be taken into custody and detained and it is for the police or for the armed forces as the case may be, to carry out that order. There is no provision under the Emergency Regulations in regard to the powers given to the Secretary

2423 2424

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

of the Ministry of Defence to slam down a Detention Order on any citizen of this country who has his fundamental rights guaranteed under the Constitution and more particularly Articles 12 and 13, to deprive his freedom in this manner. The Supreme Court has repeatedly asserted, “What are we doing?”, we are refusing, the Government is refusing to abide by the judgments of the apex court, the judgments of the Final Court. That is my contention. It is not going to rest here but, this Parliament has judicial powers. That is exactly where I am. If this Constitution should be respected in to the Secretary to the Ministry of Defence, however powerful he may be, I have no grouse in regard to that honourable gentleman, I have no grouse nor grievance, but the Secretary to the Ministry of Defence should uphold the Constitution for the reason that he has taken an oath under the Fourth Schedule to uphold the Constitution. That is my contention. This is a serious issue. If the Government wants us to abide by the Constitution it should uphold the Constitution. It should not violate the provisions of the Constitution, any Article of the Constitution and more particularly the Fundamental Rights enshrined in the Constitution. Sri Lanka had acceded to the Human Rights Conventions of 1966 and also to the First Optional Protocol to the International Covenant on Civil and Political Rights and where are we now? That is my contention. The Secretary to the Ministry of Defence cannot act mechanically. There should be reasonable information, there should be reasonable suspicion, credible information. People are arrested, put into vans or buses, brought into police stations, locked up and I find Hon. Mr. Deputy Speaker, that some of these people were shifted from certain police stations to the detention camp, particularly Boossa for the reason that there was lack of accommodation. This is the situation. This is a tragedy. This is how my Friends in the JVP were treated, tortured, killed, massacred. Tamil youth were done to death, massacred. Again we have that chapter unfolding. Therefore Mr. Deputy Speaker thanking you for this opportunity, I dare say it is not too late for the Government to accept and release them. Please release them in the name of the Constitution. This Constitution as long as it is there should be upheld by all of us. I talk on the basis of Constitutional Rights and in the name of the Constitution. In the name of Fundamental Rights enshrined in the Constitution, I call upon the Government to act now though it is late. It is better to be late than never. My good Friend, the Hon. Thurairetnasingam I do believe and I do hope and I am very proud to say would second my Motion. I thank you, Mr. Deputy Speaker.

ගරු ෙක්. තුෙරයිෙරට්නසිංගම් මහතා மாண்ᾗமிகு க. ᾐைரெரட்ணசிங்கம்) (The Hon. K. Thurairetnasingam) ெகளரவ பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, தமிழ்த் ேதசியக் கூட்டைமப்ைபச் ேசர்ந்த எமᾐ சேகாதர பாராᾦமன்ற உᾠப்பினர் ெகளரவ என். ᾯ காந்த அவர்கள் ᾙன்ெமாழிந்த இந்த ஒத்திைவப்ᾗப் பிேரரைணைய நான் ᾙற்ᾠᾙᾨதாக ஆதாித்ᾐ வழிெமாழிகின்ேறன். கடந்த சில தினங்களாக - නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) Thank you. Hon. Member, the fifteen minutes allotted to the Opposition has already been utilized - [Interruption.] Only fifteen minutes was allocated. ගරු ෙක්. තුෙරයිෙරට්නසිංගම් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு க. ᾐைரெரட்ணசிங்கம்) (The Hon. K. Thurairetnasingam) Thank you. ගරු රත්නසිරි විකමනායක මහතා (අගාමාතɕතුමා, අභɕන්තර පරිපාලන අමාතɕතුමා සහ රාජɕ ආරක්ෂක, මහජන ආරක්ෂාව, නීතිය හා සාමය පිළිබඳ නිෙයෝජɕ අමාතɕතුමා)

(மாண்ᾗமிகு ரத்னசிறி விக்கிரமநாயக்க - பிரதம அைமச்சᾞம் உள்ளக நிᾞவாக அைமச்சᾞம் பாᾐகாப்ᾗ, ெபாᾐமக்கள் பாᾐகாப்ᾗ, சட்டᾙம் ஒᾨங்கும் பற்றிய பிரதி அைமச்சᾞம்) (The Hon. Ratnasiri Wickramanayaka - Prime Minister, Minister of Internal Administration and Deputy Minister of Defence, Public Security, Law and Order) ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ගරු ශී කාන්තා මන්තීතුමා, සභාව තැබීෙම් ෙයෝජනාව ඉදිරිපත් කරමින් කළ කථාවට මම ඉතාමත්ම ඕනෑකමින් සවන් දී ෙගන සිටියා. අපි සාමානɕ නීතිය පවත්වන ෙවලාවක ද ෙම් අද ලංකාව තිෙබන්ෙන්? එවැනි අවස්ථාවක් ෙනොමැති විටක දී කියා කළ යුතු ආකාරය ෙම් ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාෙවන්ම කියා තිෙබනවා. සාමානɕෙයන් ෙම් රෙට් සාමය තිෙබන ෙවලාවක නම්, ෙබෝම්බ පිපිෙරන්ෙන් නැති ෙවලාවක නම්, මිනිස්සු මරන්ෙන් නැති ෙවලාවක නම්, එෙහ ෙමෙහ අපරාධ කරන්ෙන් නැති ෙවලාවක නම්, ඒ නීතිය ඒ ආකාරෙයන් කියාත්මක කළ හැකි බව මම පිළිගන්නවා. ඒෙක් කිසිම ගැටලුවක් නැහැ. නමුත් එෙහම තත්ත්වයක් ෙනොෙවයි, අද ලංකාෙව් තිෙබන්ෙන්. ෙම් ඊෙය් ෙපෙර්දාත් නුෙග්ෙගොඩ සිද්ධියක් ඇති වුණා තමුන්නාන්ෙසේට මතක ඇති. ගරු ඩග්ලස් ෙද්වානන්ද අමාතɕතුමාෙග් අමාතɕාංශෙය් දී එවැනි සිද්ධියක් ඇති වුණා. ඒ ආකාරෙය් සිද්ධීන් ඇති ෙවන ෙකොට කුමන ආකාරෙයන් කියා කළ යුතු ද කියා ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාෙවන්ම විධිවිධාන සලසා දී තිෙබනවා. ඒ තමයි, හදිසි නීතිය පකාශයට පත් කිරීෙමන් සාමානɕ නීතිය නවත්වා, හදිසි නීතිය උපෙයෝගී කර ගැනීම. අන්න ඒ වගන්ති යටෙත්යි අපි කියා කර තිෙබන්ෙන්. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාවට පටහැනිව ෙනොෙවයි; ආණ්ඩුකම වɕවස්ථාව අනුව දුන්නා වූ බලතල ෙම් පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව පාවිච්චි කර තිෙබනවා. ජනාධිපතිතුමා විසින් පනවන ලද ඒ නිෙයෝග හදිසි නීතිය යටෙත් අපි කියාත්මක කර තිෙබනවා. අපි කිසිම ජාතිවාදී වැඩ පිළිෙවළකට ගිෙය් නැහැ. සැක කරන පුද් ගලයන් අරෙගන අපි පශ්න කළා. මම නැහැයි කියන්ෙන් නැහැ. මම තමුන්නාන්ෙසේට ඒ සංඛɕා ෙල්ඛන ෙදන්නම්. අපි පශ්න කරන්නට 2,554 ෙදෙනක් ගත්තා. අපි ඒ 2,554න් 1,559 ෙදෙනක් එෙවෙල්ම, ක්ෂණිකව, පැය ෙදක තුනක් ඇතුළත නිදහස් කළා. ෙපොලීසියටවත් ෙගන යන්ෙන් නැතිව ඒ ගත් තැන්වලදීම පශ්න කර ඒ අයව නිදහස් කර හැරියා. ඉන් පසුව

2425 2426

[ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා]

2007 ෙදසැම්බර් 05

ෙපොලීසියට ෙගන ෙගොස් පශ්න කර සෑහීමට පත් වුණායින් පසුව 390 ෙදෙනක් නිදහස් කළා. ඊ ළඟට 102කට ඒ ෙගොල්ලන්ෙග් අනනɕතාව සනාථ කරන්න, ඔප්පු කරන්න බැරි වුණා. ඒ අයෙග් අනනɕතාව සම්බන්ධව තවදුරටත් ෙතොරතුරු සපයා දීමට අවශɕ ෙව්ලාව ලබා දීම පිණිස උසාවියට ඉදිරිපත් කර රිමාන්ඩ් භාරෙය් තැබුවා. ඉන් අනතුරුව ඉතිරි වුණු 100 ෙදෙනකු අපි රඳවා ගැනීෙම් නිෙයෝග යටෙත් රඳවා ෙගන ඉන්නවා. ඒ අය LTTE එකට සම්බන්ධතාවක් තිෙබනවාය කියා අෙප් බුද්ධි අංශය විසින් අපට ෙතොරතුරු ලබා දී තිෙබනවා. එම නිසයි අපි රඳවා ගැනීෙම් නිෙයෝග ලබා ෙගන ඒ අයෙගන් පශ්න කිරීම ආරම්භ කර තිෙබන්ෙන්. ඒ අයෙගන් පශ්න කිරීෙම් පතිඵලයක් හැටියට, පසු ගිය පැය 24 ඇතුළත වූ ෙනොෙයක් ෙනොෙයක් සිද්ධීන් සම්බන්ධව, ඇති කළා වූ සිද්ධීන් සම්බන්ධව, ඇති වුණා වූ සිද්ධීන් සම්බන්ධව සමහර ෙතොරතුරු අපට ලබා ගන්න පුළුවන් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. LTTE එකත් එක්ක තිෙබන සම්බන්ධතාව පිළිබඳව බුද්ධි අංශ විසින් දුන්නා වූ ෙතොරතුරු අනුව රඳවා ගත යුතුයි කියන පදනෙම් සිට ගත් අය පමණයි අප රඳවා ෙගන ඉන්ෙන්. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, සෑම ෙදනාම ආරක්ෂා කරන්න, හැකි තරම් දුරට ලංකාෙව් තිෙබන්නා වූ සාධාරණ නීතියට, සාධාරණ යුක්තියට අනුව හැකි තරම් දුරට අයුක්තියක් ෙනොවන ෙසේ ආණ්ඩු කරන්න රජයට යුතුකමක් තිෙබනවා. ෙකෙනක් තවත් ෙකෙනකුෙග් ජීවිතයක් බලහත්කාරෙයන් ගන්නවාට අපි කැමති නැහැ. ඒක අසාධාරණ වැඩක්. ෙකෙනකුට තවත් ෙකෙනකුෙග් ජීවිතයක් ගන්න ෙමොන අයිතිය ද තිෙබන්ෙන්? එවැනි ෙද් සිදු වීම වැළැක්වීම සඳහා අපි ෙම් ආකාරෙයන් පියවර ගත් එක ඇත්ත. අපි රජයක් හැටියට එවැනි පියවර ගන්න ඕනෑ.

ලංකාෙව් විතරක් ෙනොෙවයි, ෙවනත් රටවලත් සාමානɕ නීතිය කඩා වැටුණායින් පස්ෙසේ ෙම් ආකාරෙය් කියාදාමයන්වලට ගිහින් තිෙබනවා. එංගලන්තෙය්ත් ගිහින් තිෙබනවා. ඒක රහසක් ෙනොෙවයි. එම නිසා ෙම් රෙට් තව දුරටත් අයුක්ති සහගත වැඩවලින් ජීවිත නැති කිරීෙම් වැඩ පිළිෙවළ තුරන් කිරීම සඳහා අපිත් ෙම් කියාදාමෙය් ඉන්නවා. අන්න ඒ ස්ථාවරෙය් ඉඳලයි අපි කියා කෙළේ කියන එක මම තමුන්නාන්ෙසේට පැහැදිලිව කියනවා. අපි කිසිම ෙකෙනකුට අසාධාරණයක් කරන්න සූදානම් නැහැ. පශ්න කර අවසන් වුණාට පසුව ඒ අය නිර්ෙදෝෂීයි කියා අපට ෙත්ෙරනවා නම් ඒ අය නිදහස් කරන්න අපි සූදානම්. ස්තුතියි. පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව ඊට අනුකූලව අ. භා. 5.20 ට, 2007 ෙනොවැම්බර් 29 වන දින සභා සම්මතිය අනුව 2007 ෙදසැම්බර් 06 වන බහස්පතින්දා පු.භා. 9.30 වන ෙතක් කල් ගිෙය්ය. அதன்பᾊ பி. ப. 5.20 மணிக்கு பாராᾦமன்றம், அதனᾐ 2007 நவம்பர் 29 ஆந் திகதிய தீர்மானத்திற்கிணங்க, 2007 ᾊசம்பர் 06, வியாழக்கிழைம ᾙ.ப. 9.30 மணிவைர ஒத்திைவக்கப்பட்டᾐ.

Adjourned accordingly at 5.20 p.m. until 9.30 a.m. on Thursday 06th December, 2007 pursuant to the Resolution of Parliamnet of 29th November, 2007.

2427 2428

குறிப்ᾗ

உᾠப்பினர் இᾠதிப் பதிப்பிற் ெசய்யவிᾞம்ᾗம் பிைழ திᾞத்தங்கைளத் தமᾐ பிரதியில் ெதளிவாகக் குறித்ᾐ அதைனப் பிைழ

திᾞத்தப்படாத பிரதி கிைடத்த இᾞ வாரங்கᾦள் ஹன்சாட் பதிப்பாசிாியᾞக்கு அᾔப்ᾗதல் ேவண்ᾌம்.

සැ.යු. ෙමම වාර්තාෙව් අවසාන මුදණය සදහා ස්වකීය නිවැරදි කළ යුතු තැන් දක්වනු රිසි මන්තීන් මින් පිටපතක් ෙගන නිවැරදි කළ යුතු ආකාරය එහි පැහැදිලිව ලකුණු ෙකොට, පිටපත ලැබී ෙදසතියක් ෙනොඉක්මවා හැන්සාඩ් සංස්කාරක ෙවත ලැෙබන ෙසේ එවිය යුතුය.

NOTE Corrections which Members suggest for the Final Print should be clearly marked in their copy and sent to be Editor of HANSARD within tow weeks of receipt of the uncorrected copy. Contents of Proceedings : From 9.30 a.m. to 5.18 p.m. on 05.12.2007 Final set of manuscripts Received from Parliament : 1.45 p.m. on 21.02.2008 Printed copies dispatched : 25.02.2008 Morning

சந்தா ; ஹன்சாட் அதிகார அறிக்ைகயின் வᾞடாந்த சந்தா ᾟபா 2,178. ஹன்சாட் தனிப்பிரதி ᾟபா 18.15. தபாற் ெசலᾫ ᾟபா 2.50. வᾞடாந்த சந்தா ᾙற்பணமாக அத்தியட்சகர், அரசாங்க ெவளியீட்டᾤவலகம், இல. 132, மாயா அெவனிᾜ, கிᾞளப்பைன, ெகாᾨம்ᾗ 5 என்ற விலாசத்திற்கு அᾔப்பி பிரதிகைளப் ெபற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளலாம். ஒவ்ேவாராண்ᾌம் நவம்பர் 30 ஆந் ேததிக்கு ᾙன் சந்தாப் பணம் அᾔப்பப்பட ேவண்ᾌம். பிந்திக் கிைடக்கும் சந்தா விண்ணப்பங்கள் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்படமாட்டா.

දායක මුදල්: පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු විවාද වාර්තාවල වාර්ෂික දායක මිල රු.2178කි. පිටපතක් ෙගන්වා ගැනීම අවශɕ නම් ගාස්තුව රු. 18.15කි. තැපැල් ගාස්තුව රු. 2.50කි. ෙකොළඹ 5, කිරුළපන, මායා මාවත. අංක 132 රජෙය් පකාශන කාර්යාංශෙය් අධිකාරී ෙවත සෑම වර්ෂයකම ෙනොවැම්බර් 30දා ට පථම දායක මුදල් ෙගවා ඉදිරි වර්ෂෙය් දායකත්වය ලබාෙගන විවාද වාර්තා ලබාගත හැකිය. නියමිත දිෙනන් පසුව එවනු ලබන දායක ඉල්ලුම්පත් භාරගනු ෙනොලැෙබ්.

Subscription : The annual subscription for Official Report of Hansard is Rs. 2,178. A single copy of Hansard is available for Rs. 18.15. (Postage Rs. 2.50) Copies can be obtained by remitting in advance an annual subscription fee to the SUPERINTENDENT, GOVERNMENT PUBLICATION BUREAU, No. 132, Maya Avenue, Kirulapone, Colombo 5. The fee should reach him on or before November 30 each year . Late application for subscriptions will not be accepted.

ශී ලංකා රජෙය් මුදණ ෙදපාර්තෙම්න්තුෙව් මුදණය කරන ලදී.
